 yah acount kisi news channel,artist,netaa aadi ke soshal media acount jaise dikhte he lekin hote nakli he

 ) navaratri kaa parv najadik he, is saal 21 sitambar se sharad navaratri kii shuruuaat hogi
 In this festival lasting nine days, various forms of Goddess Durga are worshiped, this festival represents the victory of good over evil
 is dauraan log vrath main satvik bhojan ke saath-saath saaf safai aadi kai chizon kaa paalan karte hai
 At the same time there is a change of seasons
 navaratri ke dauraan anaaj (genhu or chaaval), namak, maansahaari bhojan, sharaab, pyaaj, lahasun ke alaava kai anya chizon ke seven ko varjit mana jaataa he
 But the question here is a morning cup of coffee and tea? Is it allowed in Navratri? is sawaal kaa jawaab itnaa aasaan nahin he
 Many believe that only tea can be consumed during the fast, but coffee drinkers are against this argument
 vahiin kuch log aise bhi hai jo yah maanate hai ki upwas ke dauraan chaay or coffee donon kaa seven kiya ja saktaa he
 Famous food writer Anuthi Vishal says nothing has been written anywhere about the rules of fasting for Navratri
 har insaan kii apni ek vyaktigat pasand hoti he
 Many years ago, people made such rules
 navaratri vah samay he jisamen maansahaari bhojan or anaaj kaa seven na karke vyakti apane sharir ko shuddh karata he
 So beverages like tea and coffee can be consumed during this time
 dilli kii rahane vaali shalini nandwani kaa kahana he ki vah pichley 20 saalon se navaratri ke vrath rakh rahi he or unke ghar main navaratri upwas ke dauraan chaay or coffee donon pine kii anumati he
 Buttermilk and fruit juice are also consumed along with it, but packed juices and other gas-mixed beverages are not consumed
 kya navaratri main coffee ke seven kii anumati he? Madhu Bhasin, who is a housewife, says that she has been observing Navratri fast for years and she consumes tea and coffee during this time
 hamaari koshish yahi hoti he ki packed or processd peya padaarth kaa seven na kiya jaae kyonki unamem kai kritrim agent hote hai
 Housewife Sarabjit Singh says that coffee may have a high caffeine content, but it is not known why coffee is skipped during Navratri
 kaaphi samay pehle coffee bharat main bahut zyada lokapriy nahin thi or yah abhi bhi chaay ke mukaable nahin he
 i doubt that there is any rule regarding this in Navratri
 har vyakti kii apni pasand he

 The new law on child labor has been approved by President Pranab Mukherjee and now a person appointing a child below 14 years for any work will be punished with imprisonment of up to two years and a maximum fine of Rs 50,000
 
 haalanki, skool se baad ke samay main apane parivaar kii madad karne vaale bachche ko is kanoon ke daayre main nahin rakhaa gaya he
 The new law prohibits the employment of a teenager between 14 and 18 years of age in hazardous works such as mines and other flammable substances or explosives
 haalanki, nayaa kanoon filmon, vigyapanon yaa tivi udyog main bacchon ke kaam par lagu nahin hota
 Officials said that the President gave his approval on the Child Labor (restriction and Regulation) Amendment Act, 2016 on Friday and the law has been notified
 naye kanoon ke jariye bal shram (pratibandh evam niyaman) adhinium 1986 main sanshodhan kiya gaya he taaki kisi kaam main bacchon ko niyukt karne vaale vyakti par jurmaana ke alaava sajaa bhi badhaai ja sake
 The amended law empowers the government to periodically inspect such places and places with hazardous functions where the employment of children is prohibited
 is silsile main ek vidheyak ko loksabhaa ne 26 july ko paarit kiya tha jabaki rajyasabha ne use 19 july ko paarit kiya
 Punishment for those violating it has been enhanced through the amended Act
 bacchon ko rojgaar dene waalon ko ab chah maheene se do saal kii jail kii sajaa hogi yaa 20,000 se lekar 50,000 rupee tak kaa jurmaana, yaa donon lag sakegaa
 Earlier there was a provision of punishment ranging from three months to one year and fine ranging from Rs 10,000 to 20,000 or both
 tippaniyan For the second time, the employer has been provided with a sentence of imprisonment ranging from one year to three years for being found involved in the crime
